The impact of battered women's syndrome on a person's mental state can affect their decision-making abilities, making it difficult for them to perceive threats accurately and respond to them in a rational manner. In this case, the wife's actions, such as hiring a hit man to kill her husband, may have been influenced by the psychological effects of the abuse she endured over time. Therefore, it is important for the judge to consider the battered women's syndrome in this case to provide a more comprehensive understanding of the wife's actions and intentions. This will help the jury to make a more informed decision based on the psychological impact of long-term abuse on the wife's mental state and decision-making process.
